create_trade_post = {
	set_variable = {
		name = current_trade_post_level
		value = 0
	}
	every_scope_building = {
		limit = {
			is_building_type = building_trade_post
		}
		state = {
			change_variable = {
				name = current_trade_post_level
				add = prev.level
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_building = building_trade_post
			var:current_trade_post_level > var:trade_post_level
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = num_accumulate
			}
			change_variable = {
				name = num_accumulate
				add = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					var:num_accumulate = 4
				}
				remove_variable = num_accumulate
				remove_building = building_trade_post
				set_variable = {
					name = current_trade_post_level
					value = var:trade_post_level
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = {
				name = num_accumulate
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_building = building_trade_post
		}
		remove_variable = num_accumulate
		set_variable = {
			name = current_trade_post_level
			value = var:trade_post_level
		}
	}
	switch = {
		trigger = var:trade_post_level
		1 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 1}}
		2 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 2}}
		3 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 3}}
		4 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 4}}
		5 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 5}}

		10 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 10}}
		11 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 11}}
		12 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 12}}
		13 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 13}}
		14 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 14}}
		15 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 15}}
		16 = {create_building = {building = building_trade_post level = 16}}
